      <article class="boxed push-down-45 post-1117 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-engineering tag-chat tag-sendbird tag-tutorial tag-javascript-sdk tag-react-native tag-messenger"> 
       <div class="meta"> 
        <a href="https://blog.sendbird.com/tutorial-build-a-messaging-app-using-react-native/" class="link--no-border"><img width="1126" height="493" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Build-a-messaging-app-using-react-native.png" class="attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="Build-a-messaging-app-using-react-native"></a> 
       </div> 
       <!-- Start of the blogpost --> 
       <div class="row"> 
        <div class="col-xs-10  col-xs-offset-1"> 
         <!-- Start of the content --> 
         <div class="post-content  post-content--narrow"> 
          <h1 class="entry-title  post-content__title  h2"> <a href="https://blog.sendbird.com/tutorial-build-a-messaging-app-using-react-native/">Tutorial: Build a Messaging App Using React Native</a> </h1> 
          <div class="entry-content  post-content__text"> 
           <h1>Build a Messaging App Using React Native using SendBird</h1> 
           <h4><span style="color: #ff0000;">This tutorial is based on SDK 2.0 outdated as of Sep.&nbsp;2016. &nbsp;</span><span style="color: #ff0000;">Please refer to the updated sample built with&nbsp;<a style="color: #ff0000;" href="https://github.com/smilefam/SendBird-Javascript">SDK 3.0 here</a></span></h4> 
           <p><a href="http://facebook.github.io/react/index.html">React</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/">React Native</a>&nbsp;is gaining a lot of momentum these days. For this tutorial, we’ll quickly build a messaging app using React Native with SendBird’s&nbsp;<a href="https://github.com/smilefam/SendBird-SDK-JavaScript">JavaScript SDK</a>.</p> 
           <h2>1. React Native’s Strengths</h2> 
           <p><a href="http://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/reactive-native.png" data-rel="lightbox-gallery-bGlnaHRib3gtMA==" title=""><img class="aligncenter wp-image-1072 size-full" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/reactive-native.png" alt="React Native" width="800" height="427"></a></p> 
           <p>Most of the apps today are built natively&nbsp;but, hybrid apps are developed using Webviews, so&nbsp;they have been limited in&nbsp;what properties&nbsp;and&nbsp;features they can use compared to the native counterparts. By&nbsp;using React&nbsp;Native, we can overcome these shortcomings of hybrid apps and utilize the native apps’ properties.</p> 
           <figure id="attachment_1074" style="width: 943px" class="wp-caption aligncenter">
            <img class="wp-image-1074 size-full" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/react-native-datepicker.png" alt="React Native - DatePicker" width="943" height="240">
            <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
             http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/datepickerios.html#content
            </figcaption>
           </figure> 
           <p>Apps developed using Webviews are also quite slow compared to the native apps. React Native separates out the JavaScript codes and the native codes into different threads, and the communication between the two are done asynchronously&nbsp;resolving the&nbsp;slow speed issue. This results in&nbsp;faster performance compared to the hybrid apps.</p> 
           <p>Finally, React Native can be developed using JavaScript, so if you are new to the native app development, you can use your existing knowledge and experience to ramp up your development speed.</p> 
           <p>React Native is already being used by&nbsp;<a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/facebook-groups/id931735837">Facebook Group&nbsp;iOS App</a>&nbsp;and Facebook Ads Manager (<a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.facebook.adsmanager">Android</a>, <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/facebook-ads-manager/id964397083">iOS</a>).</p> 
           <figure id="attachment_1075" style="width: 699px" class="wp-caption aligncenter">
            <img class="wp-image-1075 size-full" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/react-native-facebook-group.png" alt="Facebook Apps using React Native" width="699" height="635">
            <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
             https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/facebook-groups/id931735837
            </figcaption>
           </figure> 
           <h2>2. React Native Tutorial with SendBird JavaScript SDK</h2> 
           <p>This tutorial is composed&nbsp;of&nbsp;four pieces:</p> 
           <ol> 
            <li><strong>React Native&nbsp;Environment Setup</strong></li> 
            <li><strong>Login Feature</strong>&nbsp;– 1) The screen, 2) The inputs, 3) Debugging 4)&nbsp;Logging into SendBird</li> 
            <li><strong>Channel List Feature</strong>&nbsp;– 1) The screen, 2) Getting the channel list, 3)&nbsp;Entering a&nbsp;channel</li> 
            <li><strong>The Messaging&nbsp;Feature</strong>&nbsp;– 1) The screen, 2) The inputs and the back button, 3) Sending and receiving&nbsp;messages</li> 
           </ol> 
           <p>* The final output of this tutorial can be downloaded <a href="https://github.com/smilefam/SendBird-JavaScript/tree/master/tutorial-react-native-sample/SendBirdSample">here</a>.</p> 
           <figure id="attachment_1100" style="width: 1014px" class="wp-caption aligncenter">
            <img class="wp-image-1100 size-full" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/sendbird.png" alt="SendBird's Official Website" width="1014" height="936">
            <figcaption class="wp-caption-text">
             <a href="https://sendbird.com/">https://sendbird.com/</a>
            </figcaption>
           </figure> 
           <h3><strong>1) React Native&nbsp;Environment Setup</strong></h3> 
           <p>You can easily get&nbsp;SendBird’s JavaScript SDK using <a href="http://bower.io/search/?q=sendbird">Bower</a> or <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/sendbird">npm</a>. You can also download from <a href="https://github.com/smilefam/SendBird-SDK-JavaScript">our&nbsp;Github Repository</a>&nbsp;as well. Using this JavaScript SDK, we’ll learn how to build an iOS&nbsp;messaging app using React Native.</p> 
           <p>We are using React Native version 0.20.0, SendBird JavaScript SDK version 2.1.6 for this tutorial. For the editor, we’re using <a href="https://atom.io/">Atom</a>, which is a decent&nbsp;editor, but you can also use your favorite editor in its place.</p> 
           <p>This tutorial was written with OS X in mind, and we are using the following functions on React Native:</p> 
           <ul> 
            <li><em><a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/navigator.html#content">Navigator</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/view.html#content">View</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/text.html#content">Text</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/image.html#content">Image</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/textinput.html#content">TextInput</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/listview.html#content">ListView</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/scrollview.html#content">ScrollView</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/touchablehighlight.html#content">TouchableHighlight</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/stylesheet.html#content">StyleSheet</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/dimensions.html#content">Dimensions</a></em></li> 
           </ul> 
           <p>Let’s setup React Native development environment. <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/getting-started.html#content">Getting Started</a>&nbsp;documentation on React Native’s official website has a great guide to help you get started.</p> 
           <p>You need&nbsp;<a href="https://nodejs.org/en/">Node.js</a>&nbsp;version 4.0 or above&nbsp;installed. To track file changes, we recommend&nbsp;installing&nbsp;<a href="https://facebook.github.io/watchman/docs/install.html">watchman</a>.</p> 
           <p>Finally, let’s install React Native using <em>npm</em>:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4bb6944078803" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">install React Native</span>

               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

              <span class="crayon-language">Shell</span>
             </div>
            </div> 
            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
npm install -g react-native-cli</textarea>
            </div> 
            <div class="crayon-main" style="">

                  <div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-59d382b4d4bb6944078803-1">
                   1
                  </div>
                 </div> </td> 
                <td class="crayon-code">
                 <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
                  <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d382b4d4bb6944078803-1">
                   <span class="crayon-e">npm </span>
                   <span class="crayon-v">install</span>
                   <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                   <span class="crayon-o">-</span>
                   <span class="crayon-i">g</span>
                   <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                   <span class="crayon-v">react</span>
                   <span class="crayon-o">-</span>
                   <span class="crayon-v">native</span>
                   <span class="crayon-o">-</span>
                   <span class="crayon-v">cli</span>
                  </div>
                 </div></td> 
               </tr> 
              </tbody>
             </table> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
           <!-- [Format Time: 0.0004 seconds] --> 
           <p>Now, we’re ready to develop using React Native!</p> 
           <p>Let’s go ahead and create a project:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4bbe038621701" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">Create React Native Project</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">

var React = require('react-native')
var {
  Navigator,
  StyleSheet
} = React;

var Login = require('./components/login');

var ROUTES = {
  login: Login
};

module.exports = React.createClass({
  renderScene: function(route, navigator) {
    var Component = ROUTES[route.name];
    return &lt;Component route={route} navigator={navigator} /&gt;;
  },
  render: function() {
    return (
      &lt;Navigator
        style={ styles.container }
        initialRoute={ {name: 'login'} }
        renderScene={this.renderScene}
        configureScene={ () =&gt; { return Navigator.SceneConfigs.FloatFromRight; } }
      /&gt;
    );
  }
});

var styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: {
    flex: 1
  }
});</textarea>

           <p>Now if you refresh the simulator (command+R), you will see a screen like this:</p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-1080" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/login-image-01.png" alt="login-image-01" width="350" height="644"></p> 
           <p>Here we’ve used&nbsp;<a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/view.html#content">View</a>, <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/text.html#content">Text</a>,&nbsp;<a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/navigator.html#content">Navigator</a>&nbsp;components and&nbsp;<a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/stylesheet.html#content">StyleSheet</a>&nbsp;API. Refer to the official documents to learn more about the details.</p> 
           <h4>2-2) The Inputs</h4> 
           <p>Here, we’ll implement a text input for receiving user’s <em>nickname</em> and the <em>login</em> button. Let’s start by editing&nbsp;<em>src/conponents/login.js</em>&nbsp;as follows, which includes many styling aspects to make it look decent enough for our tutorial:</p>

            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
var React = require('react-native');
var {
  View,
  Text,
  TextInput,
  TouchableHighlight,
  StyleSheet
} = React;

module.exports = React.createClass({
  getInitialState: function() {
    return {
      username: ''
    };
  },
  render: function() {
    return (
      &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt;
        &lt;View style={styles.loginContainer}&gt;
          &lt;TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={this.state.username}
            onChangeText={(text) =&gt; this.setState({username: text})}
            placeholder={'Enter User Nickname'}
            maxLength={12}
            multiline={false}
            /&gt;

          &lt;TouchableHighlight
            style={styles.button}
            underlayColor={'#328FE6'}
            onPress={this.onPress}
            &gt;
            &lt;Text style={styles.label}&gt;LOGIN&lt;/Text&gt;
          &lt;/TouchableHighlight&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
      &lt;/View&gt;
    );
  },
  onPress: function() {
    console.log(this.state.username);
  }
});

var styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: {
    flex: 1,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'stretch',
    backgroundColor: '#6E5BAA'
  },
  loginContainer: {
    flex: 1,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
  },
  input: {
    width: 250,
    color: '#555555',
    padding: 10,
    height: 50,
    borderColor: '#32C5E6',
    borderWidth: 1,
    borderRadius: 4,
    alignSelf: 'center',
    backgroundColor: '#ffffff'
  },
  button: {
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'center',
    borderWidth: 1,
    borderRadius: 5,
    borderColor: '#328FE6',
    padding: 10,
    marginTop: 10,
    backgroundColor: '#32c5e6'
  },
  label: {
    width: 230,
    flex: 1,
    alignSelf: 'center',
    textAlign: 'center',
    fontSize: 20,
    fontWeight: '600',
    color: '#ffffff'
  }
});</textarea>

           <!-- [Format Time: 0.0078 seconds] --> 
           <p>Just like that, we have an input field to receive the user’s <em>nickname</em> and the <em>login</em> button to start chatting:</p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-1082" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/login-image-02.png" alt="login-image-02" width="350" height="642"></p> 
           <p>Here we’ve used&nbsp;<a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/textinput.html#content">TextInput</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/touchablehighlight.html#content">TouchableHighlight</a>&nbsp;component.</p> 
           <h4>2-3) Debugging</h4> 
           <p>For us to monitor the <em>console.log()</em> that’s coded on <em>onPress</em> function, we need to open the debug window. When you press <em>Command + D</em>, you will see a screen like below:</p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-1083" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/login-image-03.png" alt="login-image-03" width="349" height="641"></p> 
           <p>When you click <em>Debug in Chrome</em>, a Chrome window will open. Here you can use the Chrome developer tools to monitor the outputs written by <em>console.log():</em></p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-1084" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/login-image-04.png" alt="login-image-04" width="676" height="195"></p> 
           <p>When you type in the <em>nickname</em>&nbsp;and click the&nbsp;<em>login</em> button, you can&nbsp;see that the value is being submitted correctly:</p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1085" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/login-image-05.png" alt="login-image-05" width="1796" height="962"></p>

           <p>and we edit&nbsp;the&nbsp;<em>onPress</em> function as follows to include necessary variables such as <em>user_name</em> and <em>guest_id</em> (a unique identifier for chat rooms) to start messaging:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4bd5591565867" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/login.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

              <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">

              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

              <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

              <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>

            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
onPress: function() {
  sendbird.init({
    app_id: 'A7A2672C-AD11-11E4-8DAA-0A18B21C2D82',
    guest_id: this.state.username,
    user_name: this.state.username,
    image_url: "",
    access_token: "",
    successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
      console.log('success');
    },
    errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
      this.setState({username: ''});
    }
  });
}</textarea>

           <p>The <em>app_id</em> used here is a pre-defined value used for our sample apps, but you can also use your own <em>app_id</em> that you get when you create a new app on SendBird’s <a href="https://dashboard.sendbird.com">dashboard</a>.</p>

           <h3>3)&nbsp;Channel List Feature</h3>

  sendbird.init({

           <!-- [Format Time: 0.0019 seconds] --> 
           <p>Refresh the simulator, type in your nickname and then push the login button. After a brief animation, you will see the following skeleton&nbsp;screen appear:<br> <img class="aligncenter wp-image-1088" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/channels-01.png" alt="channels-01" width="350" height="625"></p> 
           <h4>3-2)&nbsp;Getting the Channel List</h4> 
           <p>We’ll use a function within the&nbsp;JavaScript SDK to get the list of channels and display it to the screen we’ve just created. Edit the <em>channels.js</em>&nbsp;as follows.&nbsp;This time, it’s a pretty long code, so try to read through it to understand how it works:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4be0371390146" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/channels.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
             </div>
            </div> 
            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
var React = require('react-native');
var {
  View,
  Text,
  Image,
  TextInput,
  ListView,
  TouchableHighlight,
  StyleSheet
} = React;

var sendbird = require('sendbird');
var PULLDOWN_DISTANCE = 40;

module.exports = React.createClass({
  getInitialState: function() {
    var ds = new ListView.DataSource({rowHasChanged: (r1, r2) =&gt; r1 !== r2});
    return {
      channelList: [],
      dataSource: ds.cloneWithRows([]),
      page: 0,
      next: 0,
      channelName: ''
    };
  },
  componentWillMount: function() {
    this.getChannelList(1);
  },
  render: function() {
    return (
      &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt;
        &lt;View style={styles.listContainer}&gt;
          &lt;ListView
            dataSource={this.state.dataSource}
            renderRow={(rowData) =&gt;
              &lt;TouchableHighlight onPress={() =&gt; this.onChannelPress(rowData.channel_url)}&gt;
                &lt;View style={styles.listItem}&gt;
                  &lt;View style={styles.listIcon}&gt;
                    &lt;Image style={styles.channelIcon} source={{uri: rowData.cover_img_url}} /&gt;
                  &lt;/View&gt;
                  &lt;View style={styles.listInfo}&gt;
                    &lt;Text style={styles.titleLabel}&gt;# {rowData.name}&lt;/Text&gt;
                    &lt;Text style={styles.memberLabel}&gt;{rowData.member_count} members&lt;/Text&gt;
                  &lt;/View&gt;
                &lt;/View&gt;
              &lt;/TouchableHighlight&gt;
            }
            onEndReached={() =&gt; this.getChannelList(this.state.next)}
            onEndReachedThreshold={PULLDOWN_DISTANCE}
          /&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
      &lt;/View&gt;
    );
  },
  onChannelPress: function(url) {
    console.log(url);
  },
  getChannelList: function(page) {
    if (page == 0) {
      return;
    }
    sendbird.getChannelList({
      page: page,
      limit: 20,
      successFunc : (data) =&gt; {
        this.setState({channelList: this.state.channelList.concat(data.channels)}, () =&gt; {
          this.setState({
            dataSource: this.state.dataSource.cloneWithRows(this.state.channelList),
            page: data.page,
            next: data.next
          });
        });
      },
      errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
        console.log(status, error);
      }
    });
  }
});

var styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: {
    flex: 1,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'stretch',
    backgroundColor: '#ffffff'
  },
  listContainer: {
    flex: 11,
    justifyContent: 'center',
    alignItems: 'stretch',
    marginTop: 10
  },
  listItem: {
    flex: 1,

           <!-- [Format Time: 0.0134 seconds] --> 
           <p>You can see that the list of channels appear on your screen when you refresh it. When you scroll&nbsp;to the bottom of the list, <em>getChannelList</em> function will be called&nbsp;by&nbsp;<em>onEndReached</em> and the&nbsp;next page of the channel list will be retrieved. When you click on the channel, you&nbsp;can see the output of the channel’s URL.</p> 
           <p>You&nbsp;will see an output screen like the following if everything works correctly:<br> <img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1089" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/channels-02.png" alt="channels-02" width="1866" height="1444"></p> 
           <h4>3-3)&nbsp;Entering a&nbsp;Channel</h4> 
           <p>To see if we are indeed entering a channel correctly, let’s edit <em>onChannelPress</em> function within <em>channels.js</em>&nbsp;to retrieve the channel information as follows:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4be4264684894" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/channels.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">

               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

              <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
onChannelPress: function(url) {
  sendbird.joinChannel(
    url,
    {
      successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
        sendbird.connect({
          successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
            sendbird.getChannelInfo((channel) =&gt; {
              console.log(channel);
            });
          },
          errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
            console.log(status, error);
          }
        });
      },
      errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
        console.log(status, error);
      }
    }
  );
},</textarea>

           <p>Using the console window, you can see the&nbsp;object&nbsp;returned when you&nbsp;click on one of the channels. We’re in! ?<br> <img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1090" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/channels-03.png" alt="channels-03" width="1826" height="1416"></p> 
           <h3>4)&nbsp;The Messaging Feature</h3> 
           <p>Now for the main dish, we’re going to create our chat screen. We’ll be creating a simple, text-based chat screen like good ol’ IRC to see if this thing really works. Feel free to customize it to your liking!</p> 
           <h4>4-1)&nbsp;The Screen</h4> 
           <p>Create <em>chat.js</em> within the <em>src/components/</em>&nbsp;folder and edit as follows. This creates a raw screen like the ones we did above:</p>

           <p>We want to display the chat window when we&nbsp;click on one of the channels, so we’ll edit <em>onChannelPress</em> function within the <em>channels.js</em> file as follows:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4bec660068970" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/channels.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
             </div>
            </div> 
            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
onChannelPress: function(url) {
  sendbird.joinChannel(
    url,
    {
      successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
        sendbird.connect({
          successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
            sendbird.getChannelInfo((channel) =&gt; {
              this.props.navigator.push({ name: 'chat' });
            });
          },
          errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
            console.log(status, error);
          }
        });
      },
      errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
        console.log(status, error);
      }
    }
  );
}</textarea>
            </div>

           <p>Now when you click on a channel, you will see the&nbsp;empty chat window get displayed:</p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-1091" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/chat-01.png" alt="chat-01" width="350" height="636"></p> 
           <h4>4-2)&nbsp;The Inputs and The Back Button</h4> 
           <p>We’re almost there! To make it easier to go back and forth between the chat window and the channel list, we’ll implement the <em>back</em> button and an <em>input field</em> for sending chat messages.</p> 
           <p>Edit the <em>chat.js</em>&nbsp;file as follows:</p>

  module.exports = React.createClass({
    render: function() {
      return (
        &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt;
          &lt;View style={styles.topContainer}&gt;
            &lt;TouchableHighlight
              underlayColor={'#4e4273'}
              onPress={this.onBackPress}
              style={{marginLeft: 15}}
              &gt;
              &lt;Text style={{color: '#fff'}}&gt;&amp;lt; Back&lt;/Text&gt;
            &lt;/TouchableHighlight&gt;
          &lt;/View&gt;
          &lt;View style={styles.chatContainer}&gt;
            &lt;Text style={{color: '#000'}}&gt;Chat&lt;/Text&gt;
          &lt;/View&gt;
          &lt;View style={styles.inputContainer}&gt;
            &lt;Text style={{color: '#000'}}&gt;Input&lt;/Text&gt;
          &lt;/View&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
      );
    },
    onBackPress: function() {
      this.props.navigator.pop();
    }
  });

           <!-- [Format Time: 0.0056 seconds] --> 
           <p>When you hit the ‘&lt; Back’ button at the top left corner, <em>this.props.navigator.pop()</em> will make the current screen ‘pop’ and display the channel list screen hidden underneath.</p> 
           <p>The chat window will look&nbsp;like this:<br> <img class="aligncenter wp-image-1092" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/chat-02.png" alt="chat-02" width="350" height="641"></p> 
           <p>To start sending messages, we need to create the input text field and the ‘SEND’ button:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta -->

            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/chat.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">

            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
var React = require('react-native');
var {
  View,
  Text,
  TouchableHighlight,
  TextInput,
  Dimensions,
  StyleSheet
} = React;

var sendbird = require('sendbird');
var windowSize = Dimensions.get('window');

module.exports = React.createClass({
  getInitialState: function() {
    return {
      message: ''
    };
  },
  render: function() {
    return (
      &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt;
        &lt;View style={styles.topContainer}&gt;
          &lt;TouchableHighlight
            underlayColor={'#4e4273'}
            onPress={this.onBackPress}
            style={{marginLeft: 15}}
            &gt;
            &lt;Text style={{color: '#fff'}}&gt;&amp;lt; Back&lt;/Text&gt;
          &lt;/TouchableHighlight&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
        &lt;View style={styles.chatContainer}&gt;
          &lt;Text style={{color: '#000'}}&gt;Chat&lt;/Text&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
        &lt;View style={styles.inputContainer}&gt;
          &lt;View style={styles.textContainer}&gt;
            &lt;TextInput
              style={styles.input}
              value={this.state.message}
              onChangeText={(text) =&gt; this.setState({message: text})}
              /&gt;
          &lt;/View&gt;
          &lt;View style={styles.sendContainer}&gt;
            &lt;TouchableHighlight
              underlayColor={'#4e4273'}
              onPress={() =&gt; this.onSendPress()}
              &gt;
              &lt;Text style={styles.sendLabel}&gt;SEND&lt;/Text&gt;
            &lt;/TouchableHighlight&gt;
          &lt;/View&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
      &lt;/View&gt;
    );
  },
  onBackPress: function() {
    this.props.navigator.pop();
  },
  onSendPress: function() {
    console.log(this.state.message);
    this.setState({message: ''});
  }
});

           <p>Now when you type in some messages and hit&nbsp;‘SEND,’&nbsp;you can see your message&nbsp;output:<br> <img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1093" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/chat-03.png" alt="chat-03" width="1876" height="1422"></p> 
           <p>We’ve also used&nbsp;<a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/dimensions.html#content">Dimensions</a>&nbsp;API here to get the size of the window.</p> 
           <h4>4-3)&nbsp;Sending and Receiving Messages</h4> 
           <p>Last but not least, we’ll create the ability to send and receive messages. The default <em>app_id</em> used for this tutorial is also used by our <a href="https://sample.sendbird.com/">sample website</a> so you can use this site to see if your message is being transferred correctly. You can also <a href="https://github.com/smilefam/SendBird-JavaScript/tree/master/basic-sample">download</a> and install the sample website on your end to test it out as well.</p>

           <p>We’ll edit <em>getMessagesfunction</em> to to retrieve the messages and add them to the message list:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4bfc006923773" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/chat.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
             </div>
            </div> 
            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
getMessages: function() {
  sendbird.getMessageLoadMore({
    limit: 100,
    successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
      var _messageList = [];
      data.messages.reverse().forEach(function(msg, index){
        if(sendbird.isMessage(msg.cmd)) {
          _messageList.push(msg.payload);
        }
      });
      this.setState({ messageList: _messageList.concat(this.state.messageList) });
    },
    errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
      console.log(status, error);
    }
  });
}</textarea>

                  <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d382b4d4bfc006923773-1">

           <p>The <em>render</em> function will display the message list into rows of messages with user nicknames:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4c03988924937" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/chat.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
             </div>
            </div> 
            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
render: function() {
  var list = this.state.messageList.map((item, index) =&gt; {
    return (
      &lt;View
        style={styles.messageContainer}
        key={index}
        &gt;
        &lt;Text style={this.nameLabel}&gt;
          {item.user.name}
          &lt;Text style={styles.messageLabel}&gt; : {item.message}&lt;/Text&gt;
        &lt;/Text&gt;
      &lt;/View&gt;
    );
  });

  return (
    &lt;View style={styles.container}&gt;
      &lt;View style={styles.topContainer}&gt;
        &lt;TouchableHighlight
          underlayColor={'#4e4273'}
          onPress={this.onBackPress}
          style={{marginLeft: 15}}
          &gt;
          &lt;Text style={{color: '#fff'}}&gt;&amp;lt; Back&lt;/Text&gt;
        &lt;/TouchableHighlight&gt;
      &lt;/View&gt;
      &lt;View style={styles.chatContainer}&gt;
        &lt;ScrollView
          ref={(c) =&gt; this._scrollView = c}
          onScroll={this.handleScroll}
          scrollEventThrottle={16}
          onContentSizeChange={(e) =&gt; {}}
        &gt;
        {list}
        &lt;/ScrollView&gt;
      &lt;/View&gt;
      &lt;View style={styles.inputContainer}&gt;
        &lt;View style={styles.textContainer}&gt;
          &lt;TextInput
            style={styles.input}
            value={this.state.message}
            onChangeText={(text) =&gt; this.setState({message: text})}
            /&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
        &lt;View style={styles.sendContainer}&gt;
          &lt;TouchableHighlight
            underlayColor={'#4e4273'}
            onPress={() =&gt; this.onSendPress()}
            &gt;
            &lt;Text style={styles.sendLabel}&gt;SEND&lt;/Text&gt;
          &lt;/TouchableHighlight&gt;
        &lt;/View&gt;
      &lt;/View&gt;
    &lt;/View&gt;
  );
},</textarea>
            </div>

           <!-- [Format Time: 0.0058 seconds] --> 
           <p>Lastly, to connect to the right channel on SendBird, we’ll edit&nbsp;<em>onChannelPress</em> within <em>channels.js</em> as follows:</p>
           <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v_2.7.2_beta --> 
           <div id="crayon-59d382b4d4c07865554254" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-monokai crayon-font-consolas crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 24px; margin-bottom: 24px; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"> 
            <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
             <span class="crayon-title">src/components/channels.js</span> 
             <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 16px !important;height: 24px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
               <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
              </div>
              <span class="crayon-language">JavaScript</span>
             </div>
            </div> 
            <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 22.4px !important; line-height: 22.4px !important;"></div> 
            <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
             <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 16px !important; line-height: 24px !important;">
onChannelPress: function(url) {
  sendbird.joinChannel(
    url,
    {
      successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
        sendbird.connect({
          successFunc: (data) =&gt; {
            sendbird.getChannelInfo((channel) =&gt; {
              sendbird.connect({
                successFunc: (data) =&gt; { this.props.navigator.push({ name: 'chat' }); },
                errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; { console.log(status, error); }
              });
            });
          },
          errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
            console.log(status, error);
          }
        });
      },
      errorFunc: (status, error) =&gt; {
        console.log(status, error);
      }
    }
  );
},</textarea>

             </table> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
           <!-- [Format Time: 0.0032 seconds] --> 
           <p>If you are using the&nbsp;default <em>app_id</em>, you can connect to our <a href="https://sample.sendbird.com/">sample website</a> and see if your React Native’ app indeed sends the messages correctly.</p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1094" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/chat-04.png" alt="chat-04" width="911" height="766"></p> 
           <p><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1095" src="https://blog.sendbird.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/chat-05.png" alt="chat-05" width="849" height="759"></p> 
           <hr> 
           <p>So that’s a wrap!&nbsp;There are many more features in JavaScript SDK that has not been covered in this tutorial, so feel free to check out <a href="https://sendbird.gitbooks.io/sendbird-javascript-sdk/content/">the documentation</a> to&nbsp;build an even more advanced messaging app.</p> 
           <p>Here’s <a href="https://github.com/smilefam/SendBird-JavaScript/tree/master/basic-react-native-sample/SendBirdReactNativeSample">another sample project</a> that has a bit more in-depth features than what’s&nbsp;been covered in this tutorial.</p> 
           <p>There’s a lot more to learn about React Native, but it is beyond the scope of this tutorial. Hopefully, you got a taste of what React Native can do using SendBird JavaScript SDK. Please take a look at React Native’s <a href="http://facebook.github.io/react-native/docs/getting-started.html">official documentation</a> to build&nbsp;even more amazing apps.</p> 
           <p>If you have any questions regarding this tutorial or using SendBird in general, please drop us a note <a href="mailto:support@sendbird.com">here</a>.</p> 
           <p>Thanks! ?</p> 
          </div> 
         </div>

Just my two cents though, is that React and React native are driving ES6 forward quite hard at the moment, and the method syntax of (for example) render() { … } rather than render: function() { … } is quite a bit more succinct.
